力量的代价

返回同伴目录 | 返回卡西娅目录 | 上一章

力量的代价

The Price of Power

任务简介

卡西娅一直为家族的过去所困扰着，想要解开那些难以捉摸的谜团，找到群星圣仪的真相，弄清奥赛罗家族力量的本质究竟是什么。她希望行商浪人能跟随她看到的幻象前进，这样就能揭开奥赛罗家族过去的秘密，了解她在这个世界真正的目的。

The Lady Navigator is plagued by visions about her House's past, the Starway Atlas's creation, and the vague and elusive mystery that hides the truth about the nature of House Orsellio's power. Cassia has asked the Rogue Trader to follow her visions so that she may expose the past and understand her true purpose in this world.

目标

1. 举行仪式

标题

举行仪式

Perform the ritual

描述

为了找到通往圣仪宫殿的道路，卡西娅打算根据她看到的幻象，重现提西福涅·奥赛罗曾举行过的仪式。

Cassia intends to recreate Tisiphone Orsellio's rituals from her visions in order to find the way to the physical Palace of the Atlas.

目的地

萨马拉格斯领

Smaragdus Mundos

2. 探索神秘的世界

标题

探索神秘的世界

Explore the mysterious world

描述

通过提西福涅的仪式，行商浪人与卡西娅找到了远古的亚空间航线，来到了隐藏在亚空间风暴中的世界。这颗行星扭曲的核心中，究竟隐藏着怎样的秘密？

The ritual recreated an ancient warp route which brought the Rogue Trader and the Lady Navigator to a world hidden in the eye of a warp storm. What secret does the planet's twisted heart contain?

目的地

老妪世界

Crone World

3. 了解群星圣仪创造的真相

标题

了解群星圣仪创造的真相

Learn the truth about the Atlas's creation

描述

在这个被亚空间扭曲的世界中，行商浪人与卡西娅并没有找到要找的答案，而是找到了更多无法解释的问题。丑角剧团埋伏在这古老的艾达灵族废墟之中，这些异形与奥赛罗家族之间究竟有什么关系？

The warp-disfigured world offered more questions than answers to the Rogue Trader and the Lady Navigator. A Troupe of Harlequins was lying in wait in these ancient Aeldari ruins. What is the connection between these xenos and House Orsellio?

目的地

老妪世界

Crone World

4. 在虚空舰上与卡西娅交谈

标题

在虚空舰上与卡西娅交谈

Talk to Cassia on the ship

描述

卡西娅希望有时间能和行商浪人讨论一下在艾达灵族的远古世界中发生的事情，行商浪人可以在舰桥上找到她。

The Lady Navigator wishes to discuss all that transpired on the ancient Aeldari world once she has had time to collect her thoughts. The Lord Captain can find her on the ship's bridge.

目的地

冯·瓦兰修斯虚空舰，舰桥

Bridge, von Valancius Voidship

5. 离开这个世界

标题

离开这个世界

Leave the world

描述

行商浪人已经决定了奥赛罗家族的命运。由于擅自利用异形造物，犯下了背叛帝国的罪名，这些异端分子已经付出了生命的代价。现在，行商浪人和随行人员应该回到飞船，穿过肆虐的亚空间风暴，返回科罗努斯扩区。

The Rogue Trader has decided the fate of House Orsellio. For tampering with a xeno-artefact and betraying the Imperium, the heretics paid with their lives. Now it is time for the Rogue Trader's retinue to return to the ship and make their way back to the Koronus Expanse through the raging warp storm.

完成文本

群星圣仪秘密的真相已经揭晓。奥赛罗家族为这么多年的统治地位付出了昂贵的代价，而卡西娅也由于家族犯下的罪过，付出了同样惨重的代价。

The secret of the Starway Atlas has been laid bare, and House Orsellio has paid a high price for their years of supremacy. So has the Lady Navigator, for her family's mistakes.

场景：“住手，异形

  • “住手，异形！你不是答应过，说要杀了那个女孩和保护她的人，放过剩下的人吗？”
  • "Stop, xenos! Didn't you promise that you would kill the girl along with her protectors and spare the rest?"

  • “这是怎么回事？行商浪人和家族的叛徒沆瀣一气，把圣子引诱到了异形设下的陷阱里？我真希望是我看错了，但我现在明白了，塞蕾塔摄政王派我们跟踪你的船，这实在是个英明的决定。” / 这位身材魁梧的女性拿着手枪，但浑身散发着疲惫的迹象。她的脸隐藏在镶满宝石的三眼面具后面，精致的导航宗族外袍上留着近期战斗的痕迹，还沾着干涸的血迹。
  • "What is this? The Rogue Trader and the traitors to the House have lured the Child into a trap set by xenos? I wish my eyes were deceiving me. But now I can see clearly that Great Regent Ciretta was right to send us after your vessel." / The sturdily built woman is armed with a pistol, and yet, there are signs of exhaustion in her posture. Her face is hidden behind an encrusted three-eyed mask and her elaborate Navis Nobilite vestments are marred by dried blood and other evidence of recent combat.

  • "You will stop defiling the remains of the hallowed ground of our ancestors with your semblance of speech, mon-keigh." / The Harlequin's bright clothes glimmer faintly in the dim light of the system's star, and the sinister grin on his mask only adds to his menacing and aloof presence. / "The final act will soon unfold where you will pay for the deeds of your ancestors. Stay put and wait for the puppeteer to pull at your strings."
  • Cue_0016
  • “你竟敢威胁我，异形？” / 卡西娅的冰冷的声音响了起来，充满了残忍、无情与怨恨，你几乎认不出来。 / “这里本该是圣仪的神殿，可为什么会是异形的废墟？这个地方为什么笼罩着一层无法穿透的黑雾？回答我！”
  • "You dare threaten me, xenos?" / Cassia's ice-cold voice is completely unrecognisable. Cruel. Ruthless. Resentful. / "Why are there xenos ruins where the Palace of the Atlas should be? Why is this place coated in an impenetrable black mist? Answer me!"
  • Cue_6
  • 丑角反射性地畏缩着，但随后立刻缓和下来。 / “能看到纱芮尔的三眼猴子啊，你的祖先印下的污点，已经开始反噬你的肉体与灵魂了。你们这些可悲的愚者，总是渴望不属于你们的力量。如今唯一的仁慈，就是结束你的苦难。”
  • The Harlequin flinches reflexively but then his body instantly eases back. / "Three-eyed mon-keigh who sees into Sha'eil, the taint of your ancestors has begun to consume your body and soul. Pathetic fools with an insatiable lust for power that is not yours. Ending your misery will be merciful."

  • "Silence, traitor! The Atlas is the sacred relic of House Orsellio, it is what elevates us above the rest! How dare you—" / The regent's envoy abruptly loses her breath with a groan and she clutches her chest where her Atlas is implanted. / "I refuse... to accept this... Impossible..."

  • “像这样的行星，我们称之为‘老妪世界’。早在我的时代之前，这些世界就已经存在了。那个时候，艾达灵族还是个团结的种族，我们的帝国从银河系一端延伸到另一端。这个世界是最初恒星照耀下的世界，是从未被玷污过的世界。我从没想到，居然还能找到这样的世界。”
  • "We call planets such as this one Crone Worlds. They came to be long before my time, back when all of the Aeldari were a united people whose empire stretched from one edge of the galaxy to the other. It is a World Beneath the First Stars. An Unblighted World. I never thought that I would come to find one."

Despoiled it of its relics. Ruined all there was to the last stone. But worst of all, you sullied the souls of our ancestors reposed in their sacred vessel, the Spirit Monolith!"

  • 他纤细的手指指向漂浮在身后的古怪水晶，你周围的所有丑角都握紧了手中的武器。

  • "Like... a sea of bottomless blue..." / Cassia looks around her with a stunned expression, her gaze shifting from one xenos to another. / "I... I did not know that living things could exude such saturated hues. I wish I could paint this ocean a different colour."

  • 这块巨大的半透明石头与这里产生着奇妙的共鸣。你感觉到它散发出的力量，充满了神秘、躁动与沉静……仿佛从身体中扯出的巨型心脏一样。然而，这块晶莹剔透的石头表面却遍布着几百条暗色的纹路，仿佛某种可怕的疾病在它内部生根发芽。
  • This enormous translucent stone shares a strange resonance with this place. You can sense the energy emanating from it: mysterious, restless, coagulated... It resembles a giant heart that has been plucked out of its owner's chest. Its crystal clarity is pierced by hundreds of dark veins that have taken root within like a terrible illness.

  • Cue_24
  • “安静。” / 丑角的语气很平静，但充满了命令的意味。 / “你们这些三眼猴子能看到纱芮尔，因此你们看到了真相，我也并不意外。当我第一眼见到你们的时候，我就意识到了这一点。你们这些可怜虫，你们乞求我们，要我们帮忙消灭你们自己的同胞。我早就在你们体内感觉到了我们先祖的呼唤。我听到了他们的恳求，感觉到了他们无尽的折磨。我早就知道，你们找到了一个老妪世界。于是我谦卑地等待着，等待你们为我指路的时刻。”
  • "Quiet." / The Harlequin's tone is mild, but it is not a request. / "I am unsurprised that the truth is hidden from your gazes, three-eyed mon-keigh who see into Sha'eil. I realised it the moment I met the first of you. Wretched. Begging us to help you destroy your own kin. I sensed it within you: our ancestors' call. Their pleas. Their endless torment. I knew that what you found was a Crone World. And I humbly waited for the day you would lead me to it."

  • Cue_36
  • 伊莉耶特瞪了卡西娅一眼。 / “原来这就是原因……这就是为什么你每次出现，我的灵魂都会被挤压得像小溪中的珍珠一样，喉咙都感觉像是被荆棘缠住一样。这就是为什么你的话就像毒药一样渗入我的灵魂，留下无法愈合的伤口。因为你体内埋藏着巨型灵魂石的碎片，猴子！它遭到了扭曲，它让我的祖先遭到折磨，借此为你提供力量。”
  • Yrliet glowers at Cassia. / "So that is why... that is why your presence makes my soul shrink to the size of a river pearl and my throat choke in a collar of thorns. That is why your words seep into my soul like poison, leaving wounds that will not heal. There is a shard of the Spirit Monolith inside you, mon-keigh! Twisted. Perverted. Invigorating you by making my ancestors suffer."
  • Cue_47
  • “很遗憾，你说得没错，流浪者。那些三眼猴子的祖先打算控制巨型灵魂石的力量，但却一次又一次地失败。到了最后，他们找到了利用这种力量的方法——一种可怕的方法，一种充满痛苦、不可饶恕的方法。他们损毁了巨型灵魂石，把它化成了无数碎片，削弱了碎片中灵魂的力量，之后……” / 丑角的声音颤抖着，充满了愤怒。 / “之后，他们把巨型灵魂石的碎片放在了他们自己的身体里，强化他们的力量。”
  • "Alas, you are right, Outcast. The ancestors of the three-eyed mon-keigh sought to command the power of the Spirit Monolith, and yet they suffered failure time and again. Eventually, they discovered a way to harness this power: a terrible way, torturous and unforgivable. They shattered the Monolith into many shards and weakened the souls within. And then..." / The Harlequin trembles with fury. / "Then they placed the shards of the Spirit Monolith inside their bodies to empower their abilities."
  • Cue_0041
  • “我从来没想过，我的家族的真相居然会如此残酷……” / 卡西娅将脸埋在手里，你感觉绝望的波浪从她纤细的身体中不断蔓延，她似乎变得像玻璃一样脆弱。
  • "I never wished to learn such harsh truths about my own House..." / Cassia buries her face in her hands and you feel waves of despair spreading from her lithe frame, which suddenly appears as fragile as glass.

  • The renegade Navigator stares at Cassia in shock. / "You... you are more than just a tyrant's heir! You are a successor to a mad heretic. A betrayer of the faith! You must be destroyed. You and the Atlas. Once and for all!"
  • Cue_49
  • “你以为这个问题很容易解决，是吗，猴子？如果你们死了，你们的灵魂就会被囚禁在巨型灵魂石里。我们的祖先已经守护灵魂石太久了，当灵魂石吸收猴子的灵魂时，这个过程会腐化我们祖先的灵魂，你们的灵魂也同样如此。巨型灵魂石吸收的猴子灵魂越多……就会变得越不稳定。艾达灵族的灵魂与猴子的灵魂为了争夺主导地位，已经在这块灵魂石中跳过无数场舞蹈了。这块灵魂石正在不断变弱，你应该也已经感觉到了。”
  • "You think the solution is so easy, don't you, mon-keigh? When you die, your souls become captives inside the Spirit Monolith. This process is deranging to our ancestors, who have served as the Monolith's guardians for aeons. It is equally agonising to the souls of your dead. And the more mon-keigh souls the Monolith absorbs... the more volatile it becomes. The Aeldari and the mon-keigh have spent many a dance battling for supremacy within the Monolith, and its integrity is waning. You sense it too."

  • "I shall use the Atlas to sever my subjects' connection to the Spirit Monolith and then I shall extract its shards from every Navigator of House Orsellio. This artefact is implanted at birth, but that does not mean that the ritual cannot be reversed. I witnessed its creation through Tisiphone's eyes in my visions. I lived it, over and over again, through the memories of the Setthala clan. I... I can recreate the ritual that will return the souls of your kin to you and save my people's lives."

And the more mon-keigh souls the Monolith absorbs... the more volatile it becomes. The Aeldari and the mon-keigh have spent many a dance battling for supremacy within the Monolith, and its integrity is waning. You sense it too."

  • "I never expected to hear such words from the mouth of the cursed Child." / The Navigator slowly bows his head. / "Child... no, Lady Cassia. If such is your decision, House Orsellio will follow you. The time has come for us to do away with the dark pages of our House's history."
  • Cue_0090
  • “提西福涅用异形造物进行实验，这样的举动实在是太愚蠢了，但我们不能摧毁圣仪，至少现在还不行。奥赛罗家族和这块灵魂石一样衰弱，如果我们简简单单地摧毁了圣仪，谁知道会给所有人带来怎样的后果？我会深入研究我们家族的远古文献，探寻塞塔拉氏族的记忆……我相信，只要有足够时间，我们一定会找到办法，消灭这个曾被我们当做‘祝福’的诅咒。”
  • "It was unwise of Tisiphone to use an artefact of the xenos for her experiments, but we cannot afford to destroy the Atlas. Not at this time. House Orsellio is weakening along with this stone. Who can say what will happen to us all if we destroy it? I shall delve into our House's ancient documents and reach out to the memories of the Setthala clan... I am certain that we will find a way to rid ourselves of this curse that was once called a blessing. All in due time."
  • Cue_52
  • “够了！” / 卡西娅的红眼睛里充满了蔑视的意味，声音也一反常态地严厉。在她的注视之下，那位导航者不禁缩成一团，瑟瑟发抖。 / “为了帝国的利益，圣仪必须被保存下来！无论是塞塔拉氏族，我自己……提西福涅，还是我的无数臣民，都为奥赛罗家族的力量付出了生命的代价，我要保证他们的牺牲不会白费。”
  • "Enough!" / Cassia's red eyes are full of contempt and her voice is uncharacteristically harsh. The Navigator cannot help but shrink into a quivering ball under her gaze. / "The Atlas must be preserved and used for the good of the Imperium! The Setthala clan, myself... Tisiphone, and many subjects of mine have already paid for House Orsellio's power with their lives. And I will prove that their sacrifices were not in vain."

场景：“行商浪人

  • 对话块
  • Cue_2
  • “行商浪人？每当我出现在你面前的时候，都会很快被灰蓝色的雾气包围。” / 消沉、烦躁、失望……卡西娅刚刚进入房间，你就感觉到心中涌起一股并不属于你的情绪。 / “啊，我很抱歉，我的力量总是打算摆脱我的控制。”
  • "Rogue Trader? More often than not, whenever I find myself in your presence, greyish-blue mist surrounds me soon afterward." / Despondency. Irritation. Disappointment. The moment Cassia enters the room, you feel a wave of emotions that are not your own. / "Ah, I beg your forgiveness. My powers cannot stop trying to break free from my control."

  • Cue_0007
  • 卡西娅冷漠地耸了耸肩。 / “我之前通过圣仪的力量，与家族内所有导航者进行了交流。这段时间以来，我越来越清楚地感觉到，我们之间的联系变得越来越紧密。不过，那些叛徒又摧毁了几座虚空星站，内部冲突偶尔也会造成伤亡。奥赛罗家族神圣的血脉就这样白白流淌……这实在是令人感到遗憾。不过，考虑到你在欧拉克五号星的嗜血行为，还有你在达戈努斯官方招待会上杀害了双方领袖的冷酷决定，这样的结果并不令人意外。”
  • Cassia shrugs coldly. / "I have spoken with the House's Navigators through the Atlas. These days, I can feel with increasing clarity how our connection is growing stronger. The renegades have destroyed several more void estates, and internal skirmishes with fatal consequences are occurring on an alarmingly regular basis. Sacred Orsellio blood is being spilt... That is utterly lamentable. But unsurprising, considering your fit of bloodlust on Eurac V and your merciless actions that left not one but two leaders of the feuding sides decapitated at the official reception on Dargonus."
  • Cue_5
  • “不过，我并不是要责备你的所作所为。相反，我想告诉你的是，在穿越亚空间的过程中，我看到的幻象越来越多。同样的幻觉一次又一次出现在我眼前……我觉得我要发疯了。如你所知，那些幻象都是关于我、关于群星圣仪，以及奥赛罗家族的前任大族长提西福涅·奥赛罗。我看到了提西福涅的实验，还有关于塞塔拉家族导航者的实验。传言说，她杀光了塞塔拉家族所有导航者，因为那个家族的人不服从她的命令。”
  • "However, I am not here to reproach you for the deeds of yore. Instead, I wish to tell you of the visions that I have come to experience at an increasing rate during warp jumps. The same visions come to me again, and again, and again... It is as if I am going mad. For you see, these visions are about me, the Atlas, and Tisiphone Orsellio, the House's previous Novator. I have seen Tisiphone's experiments, the ones that involved the Navigators from the Setthala branch, which she was rumoured to have destroyed for disobedience."
  • Cue_0002
  • “但我看到的幻象，却完全不是这么回事。在我看到的景象里，是塞塔拉家族的人协助提西福涅创造了群星圣仪！实验完成之后，他们便消失不见了。或许我可以……不，我知道，只要我能从幻象中重新找到提西福涅当年的旅程，我就能找到通往圣仪神殿的道路。那里并不是奥赛罗家族的导航者看到的精神幻象，而是切切实实存在的神殿。我原本就怀疑，那座宫殿说不定真的存在，可现在……我几乎可以确定，那座宫殿就是真实存在的。”
  • "But the visions told me an altogether different story, one where the Setthalas helped Tisiphone create the Atlas! And they vanished immediately after the experiments were done with. Perhaps I can... no, I know I can find the way to the Palace of the Atlas if I recreate Tisiphone's journey from my visions. A real palace, not the psychophysical illusion to which the Orsellio Navigators can reach out. I have always had a feeling that it truly exists in our world. Now, however... I know it with absolute certainty."

I am certain that all of the House is experiencing the same, for all of us are connected. I can sense my family's fear. House Orsellio is doomed to perish in darkness should I fail to discover the reason why the Atlas is weakening. And that reason... I believe it is hidden somewhere in my visions of Tisiphone."

For you see, these visions are about me, the Atlas, and Tisiphone Orsellio, the House's previous Novator. I have seen Tisiphone's experiments, the ones that involved the Navigators from the Setthala branch, which she was rumoured to have destroyed for disobedience."
  • Cue_0002

  • "But the visions told me an altogether different story, one where the Setthalas helped Tisiphone create the Atlas! And they vanished immediately after the experiments were done with. Perhaps I can... no, I know I can find the way to the Palace of the Atlas if I recreate Tisiphone's journey from my visions. A real palace, not the psychophysical illusion to which the Orsellio Navigators can reach out. I have always had a feeling that it truly exists in our world. Now, however... 场景：“舰长大人，欧姆尼塞亚的仆人发来了紧急报告

  • "Lord Captain, an urgent report from the servants of the Omnissiah! They managed to locate a second message on the House Orsellio data-slate, hidden in the shadow of the first one. Your noble deed... gave me enough food for thought. Despite everything that transpired, I still believe we may become loyal allies to one another."

  • “您想必应该已经知道，奥赛罗家族即将召开重大会议。我们无法对这样的要求置之不理，因为哪怕这违背了我们的意愿，我们也无力反抗圣仪的诅咒。不过，如果您能说服那个该……卡西娅女士拒绝群星圣仪的力量，彻底打破束缚我们家族几百年的枷锁……我们也可以就此翻开新的一页。话虽如此，我也可以接受其他结果。比如说，假设那个被诅咒的孩子死了，我是不会为她痛哭哀悼的。”
  • "I presume you already know that House Orsellio will be holding a Grand Council in the depths of that accursed Atlas very soon. And we cannot ignore the call, for we are bound to it against our will. But if you convinced this bi... Lady Cassia to reject the Atlas and break the centuries-old shackles binding our House... We could turn over a new page. Having said that, I will accept a different outcome. Should the Child die, I am not going to shed any tears."
  • Cue_6
  • “无论您做出怎样的选择，我都愿意接受，行商浪人。我们的人已经没有什么可以失去的了，但您却可以从我们的友谊之中获益。” / 埃琳娜女士的双眼中跃动着神秘的阴影。 / “为了感谢您饶了我一命，我希望能送给您一件礼物。马提亚努斯的辉光……中有一颗翡……包裹在暴……雨的怀抱……前往……左……右……两次……之后……”
  • "I will accept any choice, Rogue Trader. My people have nothing else to lose. But you could benefit from our friendship." / There are mysterious shadows dancing in Lady Elina's eyes. / "There lies an emerald in the rays of Martianus, my gift to you for sparing my life. Head through the stor-r-ms and tor-r-rents. Le... t, ri... t, and ...wice fo... d, then..."
  • Cue_7
  • 视讯记录突然消失，通讯珠中传来了音阵大师的声音。 / “非常抱歉，舰长大人，欧姆尼塞亚的仆人再也无法抑制饥饿的机魂。希望那条视讯信息您顺利地看到了最后。”
  • The vid-recording cuts short and you hear the Vox Master's voice in your comm-bead. / "I am very sorry, Lord Captain. The servants of the Omnissiah could no longer restrain the machine spirit's hunger. I hope you were able to see the vid-message through to the end."
  • 选择 Answer_0004
  • “这恐怕不会有什么好结果，立刻毁掉数据板！”
  • "This will not end well, destroy the data-slate!"

场景：“请允许我向您报告，舰长大人

  • 对话块
  • Cue_0001
  • “请允许我向您报告，舰长大人。我们离开落脚港没过多久，一群穿着奢华制服的信使便将一个保险箱和几个带有奥赛罗家族印记的箱子送到了船上。负责运送箱子的并不是机仆，而是披金戴银的仆人……我相信，这样的做法是导航者家族奢侈的手段，试图引起行商浪人的注意。”
  • "Lord Captain, reporting. Shortly before our departure from Footfall a group of messengers in luxurious garbs delivered a strongbox and several chests bearing the insignia of House Orsellio to the ship. I suppose the use of gold-clad servants instead of servitors... was an extravagant attempt by the Navigators to draw the attention of the Rogue Trader."
  • Cue_2
  • “考虑到首都世界发生的事故，执法者对导航宗族的礼物仔细检查了三遍。我很高兴地告知您，这些箱子没有任何威胁，不会影响到您、卡西娅女士与船员的安全。话虽如此，技术人员依然检查了保险箱，在其中发现了一个数据板，里面有留给您的视讯信息，还有一部分隐藏的加密信息。我们不该擅自操作，正在等待您的指示。”
  • "Considering the incident on the capital world, the enforcer officers checked the Navis Nobilite gifts thrice. I am pleased to report that none of them threaten your, Lady Cassia's, or the crew's well-being. Having said that, a closer examination of the strongbox by the Tech-Adepts revealed a data-slate with a vid-message addressed personally to you alongside some kind of encrypted data. We dared not touch them without your instructions."
  • 选项组 Cue_2
  • 选择 Answer_0003
  • “什么视讯信息？让我看看。”
  • "What vid-message? Show me."

  • "As you command, Lord Captain." / Vigdis issues several orders, and the vid-screen of your personal cogitator springs to life, the machine innards rumbling unhappily.
  • Cue_0002
  • “您好，行商浪人。” / 沉思者的音阵系统中传来了冰冷的女性声音。你眼前出现了一个性感的女人，她的面容完全隐藏在深紫色的面纱后面。 / “我的名字叫做塞蕾塔·梅琳娜·奥赛罗。当摄政王阿伦托·奥赛罗造访您的首都世界，不幸离世之后，我有幸成为了奥赛罗家族的大摄政王。我的顾问反对我与您取得联系，然而，我们不可能忽视与圣子同行的行商浪人。” / 导航者的声音中充满了明显的敌意。

After Aaronto Orsellio's untimely demise during his visit to your capital world I was offered the honour of taking the seat of the Great Regent of House Orsellio. My advisors spoke against contacting you, but disregarding a Rogue Trader who is keeping our sacred Child by side is simply not possible." / The Navigator's voice is dripping with obvious animosity.
  • TradMessage_1
  • “奥赛罗家族不久之后会在圣仪宫殿里召开重大会议。如您所知，圣仪的力量可以连接我们家族之中所有导航者。这次会面将不会在物质世界面对面会谈，而是会在思想、梦境与幻觉的世界中进行讨论。只有通过这样的方式，才能避免流血事故，最终决定圣子的命运。”
  • "House Orsellio will soon hold a Grand Council within the palace of Atlas, the holy relic that connects all Navigators of our House. This meeting will take place not in the physical world but in the world of thoughts, dreams, and visions. It is the only way to avoid bloodshed and decide the fate of the sacred Child at last."
  • TradMessage_2
  • “幸亏有了圣仪的力量，我们能感觉到圣子的灵魂沮丧不已。不过，行商浪人的话语对圣子而言很有分量，可以安抚圣子的焦虑，引导她走上正确的道路。您可以指引她承担家族的责任，坐上家族大族长的宝座。我希望您能考虑我的提议，·冯·瓦兰修斯，因为您的能力不仅可以加强我们两个王朝之间的联系，也可以让您的王朝变得更加富庶。这条信息附带的礼物，仅仅是摄政王感激之情的沧海一粟。愿神皇保佑我们所有人。”
  • "Thanks to the Atlas we feel that the soul of the Child is full of dismay. And yet the Rogue Trader's words bear a lot of weight with the Child, so may soothe its anxiety and lead the Child down the right path. The path of accepting its duty before the House and ascending the Novator's throne. I hope you consider my offer, von Valancius, for it is in your power to not only strengthen the bond between our dynasties, but multiply your riches at the same time. The gifts accompanying this message are but an insignificant part of the Great Regent's gratitude. May the God-Emperor protect us all."
